;;; Definition of Nat and proofs of simple statements such 2 + 2 = 4 ;;

;; Knowledge base
;;; Import modules

%~ load_answer_file( '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/compat/hyperon-pln/metta/hol/NatSimpleTest.metta.answers',
%~   '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/compat/hyperon-pln/metta/hol/NatSimpleTest.metta')
;; !(import! &self Unify.metta)
;; Enumerate all programs up to a given depth that are consistent with
;; the query, using the given axiom non-deterministic functions and rules.
;;
;; The arguments are:
;;
;; $query: an Atom under the form (: TERM TYPE).  The atom may contain
;;         free variables within TERM and TYPE to form various sort of
;;         queries, such as:
;;         1. Backward chaining: (: $term (Inheritance $x Mammal))
;;         2. Forward chaining: (: ($rule $premise AXIOM) $type)
;;         3. Mixed chaining: (: ($rule $premise AXIOM) (Inheritance $x Mammal))
;;         4. Type checking: (: TERM TYPE)
;;         5. Type inference: (: TERM $type)
;;
;; $kb: a nullary function to axiom, to non-deterministically pick up
;;      an axiom.  An axiom is an Atom of the form (: TERM TYPE).
;;
;; $rb: a nullary function to rule, to non-deterministically pick up a
;;      rule.  A rule is a function mapping premises to conclusion,
;;      where premises and conclusion have the form (: TERM TYPE).
;;
;; $depth: a Nat representing the maximum depth of the generated
;;         programs.
;;
;; TODO: recurse over curried rules instead of duplicating code over
;; tuples.
;;; Collection of functions operating on numbers
;; Define max
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,max,[->,A,A,A]])
  (: max 
    (-> $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[max,X,Y],[if,[>,X,Y],X,Y])
  (= 
    (max $X $Y) 
    (if 
      (> $X $Y) $X $Y))


;; Define min
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,min,[->,A,A,A]])
  (: min 
    (-> $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[min,X,Y],[if,[<,X,Y],X,Y])
  (= 
    (min $X $Y) 
    (if 
      (< $X $Y) $X $Y))


;; Clamp a number to be within a certain range
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,clamp,[->,A,A,A,A]])
  (: clamp 
    (-> $A $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[clamp,X,L,U],[max,L,[min,U,X]])
  (= 
    (clamp $X $L $U) 
    (max $L 
      (min $U $X)))


;; Define abs
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,abs,[->,A,A]])
  (: abs 
    (-> $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[abs,X],[if,[<,X,0],[*,-1,X],X])
  (= 
    (abs $X) 
    (if 
      (< $X 0) 
      (* -1 $X) $X))


;; Define <=
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,<=,[->,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: <= 
    (-> $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[<=,X,Y],[or,[<,X,Y],[==,X,Y]])
  (= 
    (<= $X $Y) 
    (or 
      (< $X $Y) 
      (== $X $Y)))


;; Define >=
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,>=,[->,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: >= 
    (-> $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[>=,X,Y],[or,[>,X,Y],[==,X,Y]])
  (= 
    (>= $X $Y) 
    (or 
      (> $X $Y) 
      (== $X $Y)))


;; Define approximately equal

;; Nullary rule (axiom)
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[synthesize,Query,Kb,Rb,Depth],[let,Query,[Kb],Query])
  (= 
    (synthesize $Query $Kb $Rb $Depth) 
    (let $Query 
      ($Kb) $Query))


;; Unary rule
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[synthesize,Query,Kb,Rb,['S',K]],['let*',[[[:,Ructor,[->,Premise,Conclusion]],[Rb]],[[:,[Ructor,Proof],Conclusion],Query],[[:,Proof,Premise],[synthesize,[:,Proof,Premise],Kb,Rb,K]]],Query])
  (= 
    (synthesize $Query $Kb $Rb 
      (S $K)) 
    (let* 
      ( ( (: $Ructor 
            (-> $Premise $Conclusion)) 
          ($Rb)) 
        ( (: 
            ($Ructor $Proof) $Conclusion) $Query) 
        ( (: $Proof $Premise) 
          (synthesize 
            (: $Proof $Premise) $Kb $Rb $K))) $Query))


;; Binary rule
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[synthesize,Query,Kb,Rb,['S',K]],['let*',[[[:,Ructor,[->,Premise1,Premise2,Conclusion]],[Rb]],[[:,[Ructor,Proof1,Proof2],Conclusion],Query],[[:,Proof1,Premise1],[synthesize,[:,Proof1,Premise1],Kb,Rb,K]],[[:,Proof2,Premise2],[synthesize,[:,Proof2,Premise2],Kb,Rb,K]]],Query])
  (= 
    (synthesize $Query $Kb $Rb 
      (S $K)) 
    (let* 
      ( ( (: $Ructor 
            (-> $Premise1 $Premise2 $Conclusion)) 
          ($Rb)) 
        ( (: 
            ($Ructor $Proof1 $Proof2) $Conclusion) $Query) 
        ( (: $Proof1 $Premise1) 
          (synthesize 
            (: $Proof1 $Premise1) $Kb $Rb $K)) 
        ( (: $Proof2 $Premise2) 
          (synthesize 
            (: $Proof2 $Premise2) $Kb $Rb $K))) $Query))


;; Trinary rule
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[synthesize,Query,Kb,Rb,['S',K]],['let*',[[[:,Ructor,[->,Premise1,Premise2,Premise3,Conclusion]],[Rb]],[[:,[Ructor,Proof1,Proof2,Proof3],Conclusion],Query],[[:,Proof1,Premise1],[synthesize,[:,Proof1,Premise1],Kb,Rb,K]],[[:,Proof2,Premise2],[synthesize,[:,Proof2,Premise2],Kb,Rb,K]],[[:,Proof3,Premise3],[synthesize,[:,Proof3,Premise3],Kb,Rb,K]]],Query])
  (= 
    (synthesize $Query $Kb $Rb 
      (S $K)) 
    (let* 
      ( ( (: $Ructor 
            (-> $Premise1 $Premise2 $Premise3 $Conclusion)) 
          ($Rb)) 
        ( (: 
            ($Ructor $Proof1 $Proof2 $Proof3) $Conclusion) $Query) 
        ( (: $Proof1 $Premise1) 
          (synthesize 
            (: $Proof1 $Premise1) $Kb $Rb $K)) 
        ( (: $Proof2 $Premise2) 
          (synthesize 
            (: $Proof2 $Premise2) $Kb $Rb $K)) 
        ( (: $Proof3 $Premise3) 
          (synthesize 
            (: $Proof3 $Premise3) $Kb $Rb $K))) $Query))


;; Quaternary rule
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[synthesize,Query,Kb,Rb,['S',K]],['let*',[[[:,Ructor,[->,Premise1,Premise2,Premise3,Premise4,Conclusion]],[Rb]],[[:,[Ructor,Proof1,Proof2,Proof3,Proof4],Conclusion],Query],[[:,Proof1,Premise1],[synthesize,[:,Proof1,Premise1],Kb,Rb,K]],[[:,Proof2,Premise2],[synthesize,[:,Proof2,Premise2],Kb,Rb,K]],[[:,Proof3,Premise3],[synthesize,[:,Proof3,Premise3],Kb,Rb,K]],[[:,Proof4,Premise4],[synthesize,[:,Proof4,Premise4],Kb,Rb,K]]],Query])
  (= 
    (synthesize $Query $Kb $Rb

            (: $Proof1 $Premise1) $Kb $Rb $K))

          (synthesize 
            (: $Proof2 $Premise2) $Kb $Rb $K)) 
        ( (: $Proof3 $Premise3) 
          (synthesize 
            (: $Proof3 $Premise3) $Kb $Rb $K)) 
        ( (: $Proof4 $Premise4) 
          (synthesize 
            (: $Proof4 $Premise4) $Kb $Rb $K))) $Query))


;; Quintenary rule
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[synthesize,Query,Kb,Rb,['S',K]],['let*',[[[:,Ructor,[->,Premise1,Premise2,Premise3,Premise4,Premise5,Conclusion]],[Rb]],[[:,[Ructor,Proof1,Proof2,Proof3,Proof4,Proof5],Conclusion],Query],[[:,Proof1,Premise1],[synthesize,[:,Proof1,Premise1],Kb,Rb,K]],[[:,Proof2,Premise2],[synthesize,[:,Proof2,Premise2],Kb,Rb,K]],[[:,Proof3,Premise3],[synthesize,[:,Proof3,Premise3],Kb,Rb,K]],[[:,Proof4,Premise4],[synthesize,[:,Proof4,Premise4],Kb,Rb,K]],[[:,Proof5,Premise5],[synthesize,[:,Proof5,Premise5],Kb,Rb,K]]],Query])
  (= 
    (synthesize $Query $Kb $Rb

      ( ( (: $Ructor 
            (-> $Premise1 $Premise2 $Premise3 $Premise4 $Premise5 $Conclusion))

        ( (: $Proof1 $Premise1) 
          (synthesize 
            (: $Proof1 $Premise1) $Kb $Rb $K))

            (: $Proof2 $Premise2) $Kb $Rb $K))

          (synthesize 
            (: $Proof3 $Premise3) $Kb $Rb $K)) 
        ( (: $Proof4 $Premise4) 
          (synthesize 
            (: $Proof4 $Premise4) $Kb $Rb $K)) 
        ( (: $Proof5 $Premise5) 
          (synthesize 
            (: $Proof5 $Premise5) $Kb $Rb $K))) $Query))

;; Equality is reflexive.  We use === instead of == to make sure it
;; does not get reduced by the MeTTa interpreter.
;; Base case of append function definition
;; Recursive step of append function definition
;; Rule base
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,rb,[->,'Atom']])
  (: rb 
    (-> Atom))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[rb],[superpose,[[:,'EqTrans',[->,[===,X,Y],[===,Y,Z],[===,X,Z]]],[:,'EqSym',[->,[===,X,Y],[===,Y,X]]],[:,'UnaryEqStruct',[->,[===,X,X_C39_],[===,[Op,X],[Op,X_C39_]]]],[:,'BinaryEqStruct',[->,[===,X,X_C39_],[===,Y,Y_C39_],[===,[Op,X,Y],[Op,X_C39_,Y_C39_]]]],[:,'UnaryRepl',[->,[===,X,X_C39_],[Op,X],[Op,X_C39_]]]]])
  (= 
    (rb) 
    (superpose 
      ( (: EqTrans 
          (-> 
            (=== $X $Y) 
            (=== $Y $Z) 
            (=== $X $Z))) 
        (: EqSym 
          (-> 
            (=== $X $Y) 
            (=== $Y $X))) 
        (: UnaryEqStruct 
          (-> 
            (=== $X $X_C39_) 
            (=== 
              ($Op $X) 
              ($Op $X_C39_)))) 
        (: BinaryEqStruct 
          (-> 
            (=== $X $X_C39_) 
            (=== $Y $Y_C39_) 
            (=== 
              ($Op $X $Y) 
              ($Op $X_C39_ $Y_C39_)))) 
        (: UnaryRepl 
          (-> 
            (=== $X $X_C39_) 
            ($Op $X) 
            ($Op $X_C39_))))))

;; Conclusion

;;                   (=== $y $y')

;; Prove that 1 + 0 = 1
;;
;; They are many possible proof trees, the simplest one seems to be
;;
;;                                                   -----------------(Base_plus)
;;                                                   (=== (plus Z Z) Z)
;; ----------------------------------(Rec_plus)  -------------------------(UnaryEqStruct)
;; (=== (plus (S Z) Z) (S (plus Z Z)))           (=== (S (plus Z Z)) (S Z))
;; -----------------------------------------------------------------------(EqTrans)
;;                     (=== (plus (S Z) Z) (S Z))
;;
;; or in MeTTa format:
;;
;; (EqTrans Rec_plus (UnaryEqStructPres Base_plus))
;;
;; The second simplest one seems to be
;;
;;                                                -----------------(Base_plus)
;;                                                (=== (plus Z Z) Z)
;; ----------------------------------(EqRefl)  -------------------------(UnaryEqStruct)  ----------------------------------(Rec_plus)
;; (=== (plus (S Z) Z) (plus (S Z) Z))         (=== (S (plus Z Z)) (S Z))                (=== (plus (S Z) Z) (S (plus Z Z)))
;; ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------(BinaryRepl)
;;                                                (=== (plus (S Z) Z) (S Z))
;; or in MeTTa format:
;;
;; (BinaryRepl EqRefl (UnaryEqStruct Base_plus) Rec_plus) (=== (plus (S Z) Z) (S Z)))
!(synthesize 
  (: $Proof 
    (=== 
      (plus 
        (S Z) Z) 
      (S Z))) kb rb 
  (fromNumber 2))

%~ catch_warn(apply(plus,['Z',_985288,_985294])) -->
%~   error(type_error(integer,'Z'),context(system:plus/3,Context_Kw)).
%~ catch_warn(apply(plus,['Z',_1006830,_1006836])) -->
%~   error(type_error(integer,'Z'),context(system:plus/3,Context_Kw)).
%~ catch_warn(apply(plus,['Z',_1029156,_1029162])) -->
%~   error(type_error(integer,'Z'),context(system:plus/3,Context_Kw)).
%~ catch_warn(apply(plus,['Z',_9756,_9762])) -->
%~   error(type_error(integer,'Z'),context(system:plus/3,Context_Kw)).
%~ catch_warn(apply(plus,[['S',_54052],_54058,_54064])) -->
%~   error(type_error(integer,['S',_70038]),context(system:plus/3,Context_Kw)).
%~ catch_warn(apply(plus,[_78008,_78014,_78020])) -->
%~   error(instantiation_error,context(system:plus/3,Context_Kw)).
%~ catch_warn(apply(plus,[['S',_122186],_122192,_122198])) -->
%~   error(type_error(integer,['S',_138172]),context(system:plus/3,Context_Kw)).
%~ catch_warn(apply(plus,[_145514,_145520,_145526])) -->
%~   error(instantiation_error,context(system:plus/3,Context_Kw)).

%~ catch_warn(apply(plus,[_280680,_280686,_280692])) -->
%~   error(instantiation_error,context(system:plus/3,Context_Kw)).

--------------------------------------------------------------------------
;; Prove that 1 + 1 = 2
;;
;; The two simplest proof trees are the same as 1 + 0 = 1.
;;
;;
;; They are many possible proof trees, the simplest is the same as the
;; one for 1 + 0 = 1, that is:
;;
;;                                                         -----------------------(Base_plus)
;;                                                         (=== (plus Z (S Z) (S Z)
;; ------------------------------------------(Rec_plus)  ----------------------------(UnaryEqStruct)
;; (=== (plus (S Z) (S Z)) (S (plus (S Z) Z)))           (=== (S (plus Z Z)) (S (S Z))
;; ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------(EqTrans)
;;                          (=== (plus (S Z) (S Z)) (S (S Z)))
;;
;; or in MeTTa format:
;;
;; (EqTrans Rec_plus (UnaryEqStructPres Base_plus))
;;
;; This is due to the left recursive definition of plus.  The proof
;; tree of 1 + N = (S N) where N is any large number would be equally
;; simple.
!(synthesize 
  (: $Proof 
    (=== 
      (plus 
        (S Z) 
        (S Z)) 
      (S 
        (S Z)))) kb rb 
  (fromNumber 2))

%~ catch_warn(apply(plus,['Z',_369406,_369412])) -->
%~   error(type_error(integer,'Z'),context(system:plus/3,Context_Kw)).
%~ catch_warn(apply(plus,['Z',_391582,_391588])) -->
%~   error(type_error(integer,'Z'),context(system:plus/3,Context_Kw)).
%~ catch_warn(apply(plus,['Z',_413900,_413906])) -->
%~   error(type_error(integer,'Z'),context(system:plus/3,Context_Kw)).
%~ catch_warn(apply(plus,['Z',_435442,_435448])) -->
%~   error(type_error(integer,'Z'),context(system:plus/3,Context_Kw)).
%~ catch_warn(apply(plus,[['S',_480380],_480386,_480392])) -->
%~   error(type_error(integer,['S',_496366]),context(system:plus/3,Context_Kw)).

%~   error(instantiation_error,context(system:plus/3,Context_Kw)).

;; Prove that 2 + 2 = 4
;;
;;
;;                                                                          --------------------------------------------------(Rec_plus)              ---------------------------------(Base_plus)
;;                                                                          (=== (plus (S Z) (S (S Z))) (S (plus Z (S (S Z)))))                       (=== (plus Z (S (S Z))) (S (S Z)))
;; ----------------------------------------------------------(Rec_plus)  ----------------------------------------------------------(UnaryEqStruct) -----------------------------------------(UnaryEqStruct)
;; (=== (plus (S (S Z)) (S (S Z))) (S (plus (S Z) (S (S Z)))))           (=== (S (plus (S Z) (S (S Z)))) (S (S (plus Z (S (S Z))))))               (=== (S (plus Z (S (S Z)))) (S (S (S Z))))
;; --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------(EqTrans)   -------------------------------------------------(UnaryEqStruct)
;;                                    (=== (plus (S (S Z)) (S (S Z))) (S (S (plus Z (S (S Z))))))                                              (=== (S (S (plus Z (S (S Z))))) (S (S (S (S Z)))))
;; ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------(EqTrans)
;;                                                                           (=== (plus (S (S Z)) (S (S Z))) (S (S (S (S Z)))))
;;
;; or in MeTTa format:
;;
;; (EqTrans (EqTrans Rec_plus (UnaryEqStruct Rec_plus)) (UnaryEqStruct (UnaryEqStruct Base_plus)))

  (: $Proof 
    (=== 
      (plus

      (fromNumber 4))) kb rb
